        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We’re excited to announce that we’ve been named a Leader again! 
 
<a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a>, <a class="link" href="https://no.linkedin.com/company/crayon-group?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Crayon</a> and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/anglepoint-inc-?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Anglepoint</a> have been placed as a Leader in the August 2025 <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/gartner?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Gartner</a>® Magic Quadrant™ for Software Asset Management (SAM) Managed Services. 
 
In our opinion, being acknowledged as a Leader authenticates the hard work that our teams put into helping businesses around the world optimize their software investments and validates the trust that our customers place in us.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🎉 We’re proud to share that <a class="link" href="https://ca.linkedin.com/in/softwareprocurement?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Aamer Trambu</a>, Senior Consultant in our ITAM Managed Services team at <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a>, has been shortlisted as a finalist for Consultant of the Year at the <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/itam-forum?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>ITAM FORUM</a> Excellence Awards!
 
This recognition highlights Aamer’s dedication to helping our clients unlock the full value of their IT assets through expertise, innovation, and a true passion for ITAM.
 
Please join us in congratulating Aamer on this fantastic achievement, and wishing him the very best of luck ahead of the awards in November. 👏
 
You can see the full list of finalists here: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/e-TWUi2R?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/e-TWUi2R</a>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">📊 Speaker Spotlight: <a class="link" href="https://ie.linkedin.com/in/egbertij?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Egbert IJsseldijk</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/google-cloud/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Google Cloud</a> GTM Lead at <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a>.
 
“The biggest opportunity organizations miss is compounding intelligence.”
 
As Egbert explains, when sales, marketing, finance, and customer data all sit in <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsilos&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#silos</a>, innovation and efficiency stall. Connecting those data points unlocks true business outcomes and customer value.
 
At the <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a> Summit 2025 on October 23, Egbert will host “The Engine that Turns Data into Your Advantage,” exploring how an AI-native approach with analytics, ML, and agents helps organizations automate workflows, surface insights, and innovate securely at scale.
 
👉 Watch his insight now and register free for the Summit:
<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/eK-3vY9a?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/eK-3vY9a</a> 
 
Optimize today. Innovate for tomorrow.
 
<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsoftwareonesummit2025&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SoftwareOneSummit2025</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fgooglecloud&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#GoogleCloud</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fai&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AI</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fdataanalytics&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#DataAnalytics</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Finnovation&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Innovation</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🏆 WE WON!!! 🏆

What a dazzling night at the 10th Employer Brand Management Awards 2025 by <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/communicate-magazine?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Communicate magazine</a> in London.

On 24 September, <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a> proudly won:

🏅Gold: Best Employer Brand Management (Technology, Media &amp; Telecommunications).

The judges called our work “a compelling, authentic approach that balances global consistency with local relevance.”

🥈Silver Best Localisation Programme, alongside <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/amdocs?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Amdocs</a> (Gold) and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/boston-consulting-group?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Boston Consulting Group (BCG)</a> (Bronze). Judges praised it as “highly impactful and culturally attuned.”

These awards are among the most respected in the employer-branding world, judged via a rigorous evaluation process led by industry leaders.

This win celebrates the heartbeat of our brand, our stories, our videos, the vibrant <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fswocareers&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SWOCareers</a> community, and the TA campaigns that turn creativity into real career opportunities.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🚧 You can’t build <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fai&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AI</a> on shaky cloud foundations. 
 
AI can’t succeed without secure, scalable, and well-governed infrastructure in place first, and that’s where cloud landing zones come in. 

In our latest blog, we share four real-world stories that show how <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a> helped organizations build the foundations they needed for successful cloud initiatives cross <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/microsoft-azure/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Microsoft Azure</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/amazon-web-services?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Amazon Web Services (AWS)</a>, and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/google-cloud/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Google Cloud</a>.

💡 <a class="link" href="https://au.linkedin.com/company/grill'd-pty-ltd?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Grill'd</a> Healthy Burgers (<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fazure&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Azure</a>) - Cut costs by 30% while enabling secure growth and innovation. 

💡 <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/artfund?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Art Fund</a> (<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fawscloud&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AWSCloud</a>) - Implemented a compliant, secure AWS landing zone as a platform to improve stakeholder experience and resilience.

💡 Altadia Group (<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fgooglecloud&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#GoogleCloud</a>) 
Seamlessly migrated <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsap&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SAP</a> to Google Cloud with near-zero disruption, unlocking analytics potential. 

💡<a class="link" href="https://ua.linkedin.com/company/dtek?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>DTEK</a>K (AWS Cloud) 
Delivered a robust AWS landing zone to support critical infrastructure operations, setting the stage for secure, AI-enabled innovation. 

Each one story is proof that success in the cloud requires solid foundations, and AI is no exception!

This week, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/kevin-j-bernstein?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Kevin J. Bernstein</a> is shining a light from the shores of Milwaukee Harbor, standing tall in front of the iconic lighthouse, and he’s got a message for every Microsoft customer navigating today's ever-changing tech seas.

⚓ Lighthouses are there to guide ships through complex and hazardous waters....just like <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a>!

With all the <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fmicrosoft&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Microsoft</a> licensing changes, product shifts, and the rise of <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fcopilot&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Copilot</a> across the stack, it’s easy to feel a bit lost. That’s where we come in:
✅ A global partner.
✅ A steady beacon.
✅ Your guide through the storm.

Let <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsoftwareone&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SoftwareOne</a> be your lighthouse!

We’re here to help you navigate, adapt, and thrive.

🎥 Set sail with this week’s Friday Reboot and let us guide you safely to shore.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Giving back is in our DNA.

At <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a>, we’ve always believed that doing good is part of doing business. And as we continue our journey forward with <a class="link" href="https://no.linkedin.com/company/crayon-group?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Crayon</a> as one company, it’s clear that this commitment to people and communities is something we share deeply.

Through initiatives like <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsoftwareonegivesback&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SoftwareOneGivesBack</a> and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fcrayoncares&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#CrayonCares</a>, our teams around the world have supported causes that align with our values, from feeding schoolchildren in Africa and Europe, to providing trauma counselling in Ukraine, and protecting rainforests across the globe.

As one organization, we’re combining our strengths and expanding our reach, supporting global and local projects that reflect our shared ESG priorities: sustainability, inclusion, health, education, and using technology for good.

🌍 It’s not just about giving. It’s about impact.

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We are honored to be named in <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/microsoft?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Microsoft</a>’s launch of the new Microsoft Marketplace — unifying AppSource and Azure Marketplace into a single destination for cloud and AI solutions.

As our CEO, <a class="link" href="https://no.linkedin.com/in/melissa-mulholland?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Melissa Mulholland</a>, shared in the announcement:
 “This integration with the Marketplace catalog is just the beginning — we see endless potential to co-innovate and help customers navigate their AI-first transformation with confidence.”

This marks an important milestone in unlocking new routes to market and delivering more value to customers.

Read Microsoft’s full announcement here 👉 <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dS6qf_mc?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dS6qf_mc</a></p>
